Navn
Auth / Profile
Endpoint
/api/Auth/profile
Request Type GET
Fil
AuthController.cs
Rettighedd Member
er
Beskrivelse
Udskriver brugerens Rettighedder, bruges til hvad de må kunne se på
hjemmeide mm.
memberType : 1 : Member, 2 = Staff
defaultOrganisationSubGUID = Originalt organisationSubGUID for brugeren
da organisationSubGUID kan skifte hvis man skifter organisation.
additionalSub : indheolder en liste over de Organisatione ren Staff medlem
har mulighed for at skifte imellem. Hvis count = 1 er det kune ns ejen og
man har ikke mulighed for ta skifte imellem andre.
Listen er så man kan lave en drop down menu til at skifte imellem de
forskellige organisationer man har adgang til.
memberGroupWebAccessLevels : er de rettighedder brugeren har for at vise
forskellige sider i menuen på hjemmesiden.JSON Data Response
{
"memberGuid": "f062dd17-42c6-11f0-8d44-00155d0a5b1d",
"email": "kj@gidion.dk",
"name": "Kim Jørgensen",
"role": "Staff",
"organisationMainGUID": "3a649172-42c6-11f0-8d44-00155d0a5b1d",
"organisationSubGUID": "019744ea-aca8-72d1-b242-c9a6c287e1c6",
"defaultOrganisationSubGUID": "019744ea-aca8-72d1-b242-c9a6c287e1c6",
"memberType": "2",
"memberGroupWebAccessLevels": [
"1",
"2",
"3",
"4",
"7",
"8",
"9"
],
"additionalSub": {
"count": 2,
"subs": [
{
"additionalSubGUID": "019744ea-aca8-72d1-b242-c9a6c287e1c6",
"additionalSubName": "Center 1"
},
{
"additionalSubGUID": "ac125cad-476b-11f0-8d44-00155d0a5b1d",
"additionalSubName": "Center 2"
}
]
}
}

Navn
Endpoint
Fil
Rettighedd
MemberEmailVerificationCheck
/api/MemberEmailVerificationCheck/
Request
verify
Type
MemberEmailVerificationCheckController.cs
Alle
Poster
Beskrivelse
API til validering af Medlems E-Mail adresse.
Medlem vil have midtaget en mail med et validerings link. Som indheolder
et link og en Token.
Denne Token skl sendes mod dette API for at bekræfte af E-Mail bruges.
JSON Sen Data
{
"memberEmailVerificationGUID": "string"
}
Dette vil marker Medlemmet i databasen som E-Mail Verificeret og sætte
feltet i Member / MemberEmailValidated til 0
Og slette Token i feltet MemberEmailVerificationGUID så linket ikke kan
bruges mere.
JSON Data Response
{
"message": "Email verification successful",
"memberName": "Kim Jørgensen",
"memberEmail": "kj@gidion.dk",
"verified": true
}

PaymentFreePayPaymentWindowController.cs
Member
Post
Fil
Rettighedd
er
Beskrivelse
Genererer Patment Link for at Medlem kan oplyse sit kreditkort og der kan
laves første beling for Abo med de resterende dage af måneden.
JSON Data Request
{
"amount": 85
}
JSON Data Response
{
"message": "Payment link created successfully",
"paymentIdentifier": "ced4ced7-108f-4580-bb8f-d1727fca8686",
"paymentWindowLink":
"https://gw.freepay.dk/PaymentWindow/ced4ced7-108f-4580-bb8f-
d1727fca8686",
"orderNumber": "CB1013",
"amount": 85
}
Oprettes en Database Record under membercard med brugerens GUID og
diverse oplysninger for betalingen.
Når betalingen er fuldført via det oplyste link kaldes Callback adressen og
beløbet hæves og markers i dtabasen som betalt og oplysingerne er gemt til
fremtidige hævninger.Navn

Endpoint
MemberClassesListMyClasses
/api/
Request Type
MemberClassesListMyClasses
MemberClassesListMyClassesController.cs
Member/Staff
GET
Fil
Rettighedd
er
Beskrivelse
Henter de hold et medlem har tilmeldt sig i en given periode.
Hvis ingen parameter snedes med hentes data for den aktuelle uge nummer.
Med weekNumber hentes data for et specificeret uge nummer.fromWeekNumber og toWeekNumber definerer en start og slut nuge
nummer man ønsker at hente data fra.
Med startDate og endDate definers en start og slut data hvor i mellem man
ønsker at få vist data.
trainingClassClassesIsEnrolled viser om Medlem er tilmeldt dette hold eller
har anulleret sin tilmelding, True = Tilmeldt, False = Meldem har anulleret
holdet.

Navn
Endpoint
MemberClassesListAvailableClasses
/api/
Request
MemberClassesListAvailableClasses
Type
MemberClassesListAvailableClassesController.cs
Member / Staff
GET
Fil
Rettighedd
er
Beskrivelse
Viser alle Hold et medlem har mulighed for at tilmelde sig på.
Hvis ingen query data sendes med får man resultaterne for alle hold man
har mulighed for at atge bade i gen og andre centre den pågældende uge.
Parameter
weekNumber : Uge nummer der ænskes vist hold for.
fromWeekNumber, toWeekNumber : Vis hold imellem de to uge numre.
startDate, endDate Angiv slart og slut dato man vil vise mulige hold for.
orgSubGuid : Det SubGuid man ønsker at vise hold for. Hvis ikke angives
vises for alle Sub Centre man har adgang til. Hvis udfyldes vises kun for det
angivne center man angiver SubGUID for.
trainingClassTypesGUID : Hvis angives vises kun bestemte tper hold som
Cykling, Yoga mm. Hvis intet angives vises alt.
Hvis man har adgang til træning i flere centre man man få en liste over
mulige centre via allowedGuestOrganizations.
trainingClassClassesFine : 1 = Man får en bøde hvis ikke man møder op.
0=Ingen bøde
trainingClassClassesDayOfWeek : Uge dag 1 = Mandag, 7 = Søndag
trainingClassClassesAvailableSlots = Hust at checke på om der er ledige
pladser tilbage, Må ikke være 0.
trainingClassClassesAvailable = 1 Hvis derer er ledige pladser ellers 0,
bruges til at skrive sig på venteliste.
availableTrainingClassTypes : Indeholder en liste over alle mulige HoldTyper
allowedGuestOrganizations : Indholder Liste over de Centre der er
adgang til hold fra.
availableTrainingClassTypes og allowedGuestOrganizations kan bruges
til at publicere drop down bokse med så man man vælge center og
trænings type sammen med kalender for kun at få vist de trænings
typer man ønsker at se.
{

MemberClassesBookClass

{trainingClassClassesGuid}
Reque
st
Type
Pos
tFil
MemberClassesBookClassControlle.cs
Rettighed
Member/Staff
der
Beskrivelse
Medlem tilmeld sig et Hold.
Send parameter trainingClassClassesGuid som er GUID på det ønskede hold.
Er check på at Medlem ikke kan tilmelde sig flere gange.
Svar ved Booking
{
"message": "Class booked successfully",
"memberClassesBookClassGuid": "504700da-cece-4f86-bf56-
412aa724dafa",
"trainingClassClassesGuid": "56805ef4-8721-11f0-8d44-00155d0a5b1d",
"memberClassesBookClassDetails": {
"memberClassesBookClassClassName": "Straf Den Røv",
"memberClassesBookClassStartDateTime": "2025-09-02T13:00:50",
"memberClassesBookClassDuration": 45,
"memberClassesBookClassTrainerName": "Kim Jørgensen"
}
}
Svar hvis man forsøger at booke same igen.
{
"message": "You are already enrolled in this class",
"memberClassesBookClassGuid": "504700da-cece-4f86-bf56-
412aa724dafa",
"memberClassesBookClassDate": "2025-09-02T13:26:33"
}

Navn
Endpoint
StaffChangeOrganisation
/api/StaffChangeOrganisation/
change
Request
Type
PostFil
StaffChangeOrganisationController.cs
Rettighedder Staff
Beskrivelse
Bruges til at genere en ny JWT Token hvis et Staff Medlem ønsker af skifte til
et andet Center, for at ændre organisationSubGUID til den nye Center.
defaultOrganisationSubGUID forbliver hele tiden den originale
organisationSubGUID Staff brugeren hører under.
Efter genering af ny Token skal denne erstatte den Token der er gemt i
brugeren browser og siden skal fereshes så menuer mm tilpasses de nye
rettighedder.

StaffMemberList
Endpoint
/api/StaffMemberList
Request Type Get
Fil
StaffMemberListController.cs
Rettighedd Staff
er
Beskrivelse
Viser en liste over alle medlemmer i det pågældende center.
Den vil standard vise de 15 første, sorteret efter Navn, Efternavn
Det er muligt at angive antal resulater på siden med pageSize.
Set er muligt at søge i resulater med parameteret search som er en wildcard
søgning der siger at strenegen bare skal være en del af værdien i følgende
felter.
MemberFirstName, MemberLastName, MemberAddress, MemberCity,
MemberZipCode, MemberCPR, MemberPhonePrivate, MemberPhoneWork,
MemberEmail
Search = fritekst søgning
Searchmembership = GUID på medlemsskaber man ønsker at vise

Endpoint
StaffMemberManagement List Medlems Tilmeldte Hold
/api/StaffMemberManagement/
Request
member-booking-list-member-class
TypeFil
StaffMemberManagementController.cs
Rettighedd Staff
er
Beskrivelse
Henter de hold et medlem har tilmeldt sig i en given periode.
Hvis ingen parameter snedes med hentes data for den aktuelle uge nummer.
Med weekNumber hentes data for et specificeret uge nummer.
fromWeekNumber og toWeekNumber definerer en start og slut nuge
nummer man ønsker at hente data fra.
Med startDate og endDate definers en start og slut data hvor i mellem man
ønsker at få vist data.
trainingClassClassesIsEnrolled viser om Medlem er tilmeldt dette hold eller
har anulleret sin tilmelding, True = Tilmeldt, False = Meldem har anulleret
holdet.
memberGuid = GUID på medlem der ønskes vises data fra.
JSON Response Data
{
"message": "Member enrolled classes retrieved successfully",
"count": 1,
"appliedFilter": "Current week: Week 39 (2025)",
"classes": [
{
"classGUID": "392aab97-8a31-11f0-8d44-00155d0a5b1d",
"trainingClassClassesName": "Delle Blæver Del 2",
"trainingClassClassesDescription": "Delle Bllæver Del 2, ikke pive bare
klæ på",
"trainingClassClassesMax": 7,
"trainingClassClassesMin": 3,
"trainingClassClassesStartDateTime": "2025-09-25T13:34:59",
"trainingClassClassesDuration": 45,
"trainingClassClassesTrainerName": "Kim Jørgensen",
"trainingClassClassesTrainerGUID": "f062dd17-42c6-11f0-8d44-
00155d0a5b1d",
"trainingClassTypesName": "Yoga",
"trainingClassTypesDescription": "Delle Bllver Del 1, væk med de store
dæller",
"trainingClassClassesIsEnrolled": true
}
]
}Navn
Endpoint
StaffMemberManagement Vis hold en specific Medlem har
mulighed for at tilmelde sig
/api/StaffMemberManagement/
Request
GET
member-booking-list-avalible-
Type
member-class
StaffMemberManagementController.cs
Staff
Fil
Rettighedd
er
Beskrivelse
Viser alle Hold et specifikt medlem har mulighed for at tilmelde sig på.
Hvis ingen query data sendes med får man resultaterne for alle hold man
har mulighed for at atge bade i gen og andre centre den pågældende uge.
Parameter
weekNumber : Uge nummer der ænskes vist hold for.
fromWeekNumber, toWeekNumber : Vis hold imellem de to uge numre.
startDate, endDate Angiv slart og slut dato man vil vise mulige hold for.
orgSubGuid : Det SubGuid man ønsker at vise hold for. Hvis ikke angives
vises for alle Sub Centre man har adgang til. Hvis udfyldes vises kun for det
angivne center man angiver SubGUID for.
trainingClassTypesGUID : Hvis angives vises kun bestemte tper hold som
Cykling, Yoga mm. Hvis intet angives vises alt.
memberGuid : GUID på de medlem man vil vise mulighedder for. Skal
udfyldes
Hvis man har adgang til træning i flere centre man man få en liste over
mulige centre via allowedGuestOrganizations.
trainingClassClassesFine : 1 = Man får en bøde hvis ikke man møder op.
0=Ingen bøde
trainingClassClassesDayOfWeek : Uge dag 1 = Mandag, 7 = Søndag
trainingClassClassesAvailableSlots = Hust at checke på om der er ledige
pladser tilbage, Må ikke være 0.
trainingClassClassesAvailable = 1 : Det er muligt at tilmelde sig, 0 : Hold er
fyldt tilmeld via venteliste.
availableTrainingClassTypes : Indeholder en liste over alle mulige Hold
Typer
allowedGuestOrganizations : Indholder Liste over de Centre der er adgang til
hold fra.
availableTrainingClassTypes og allowedGuestOrganizations kan bruges til at
publicere drop down bokse med så man man vælge center og trænings type
sammen med kalender for kun at få vist de trænings typer man ønsker at se.JSON Response Data

skal oprettes til.

flere.

1=Monday
2=Tuesday
3=Wednesday
4=Thursday
5=Friday
6=Saturday
7=Sunday
trainingClassTemplateFrequency : Hvor tit holdet skal oprettes.
1 = Every week
2 = Every second week3 = Every third week
4 = every 4th week

Navn
Endpoint
StaffMemberPaymentGroup (List All Groups)
/api/
Request Type
StaffMemberPaymentGroup
StaffMemberPaymentGroupController.cs
Staff
GET
Fil
Rettighedd
er
Beskrivelse
List all available Payment Groups witch contains information for the
different memberships a Member can chose from.
The data is formatted for Pagination.
Their is optional information’s that can be provided if needed.
pageSize = Is the number of records that should be shows on the page, if
nothing is entered the default of 15 i chosen.
Search = Enter a search string and fin only records matching the entered
search string. If nothing is entered all i showen. It searching throu
MemberPaymentGroupName and MemberPaymentGroupDescription.
page = The page number you wnat to see the results from.
Data Descriptions
memberPaymentGroupName = Name of the Group
memberPaymentGroupDescription = Description of the Group
memberPaymentValidFrom = Date from when it should be Avalible
memberPaymentValidTo = Date from when it should be Avalible to
memberPaymentPrice = Price of the MembershipmemberPaymentPriceVAT = Is Price including VAT (True/False)
memberPaymentEnable = If the Groupe is Enabled and can be selected by
Members
memberPaymentDefault = Set to 1 if that should be selected default at sign
up.
paymentProviderDataGUID = GUID of Payment Provider
memberPaymentPausePrice = Monthly Price if a member set their
membership on pause.
memberGroupDefaultGroupsGUID = GUID of default Group member should
be assigned to if the have this membership.
API StaffListMemberGroupDefaultGroups and
StaffListPaymentProviderData contains the name and GUID witch can be
used to show the available items.
JSON Response Data
{
"message": "Member payment group list retrieved successfully",
"search": "",
"pagination": {
"currentPage": 1,
"pageSize": 15,
"totalRecords": 2,
"totalPages": 1,
"hasNextPage": false,
"hasPreviousPage": false
},
"count": 2,
"paymentGroups": [
{
"memberPaymentGroupGUID": "a68d5819-78e7-11f0-8d44-
00155d0a5b1d",
"memberPaymentGroupName": "Center 1 Payment Premium",
"memberPaymentGroupDescription": "Premium Abo. der indeholder
både normal træning og holdtræning.",
"memberPaymentValidFrom": "2025-06-06T00:00:00",
"memberPaymentValidTo": "2028-06-06T00:00:00",
"memberPaymentPrice": 150,
"memberPaymentPriceVAT": 0,
"memberPaymentEnable": 1,
"memberPaymentDefault": 1,"paymentProviderDataGUID": "3df28dda-78fe-11f0-8d44-00155d0a5b1d",
"memberPaymentPausePrice": null,
"memberGroupDefaultGroupsGUID": "790aa93e-83e4-11f0-8d44-
00155d0a5b1d"
},
{
"memberPaymentGroupGUID": "a262480c-78e7-11f0-8d44-
00155d0a5b1d",
"memberPaymentGroupName": "Center 1 Payment Standard",
"memberPaymentGroupDescription": "Standard Abo. der kun indeholder
træning",
"memberPaymentValidFrom": "2025-06-06T00:00:00",
"memberPaymentValidTo": "2028-11-06T00:00:00",

Endpoint
StaffAccessManagementStaffGroup (Create new StaffGroup)
/api/StaffAccessManagementStaffGroup/
Request
POST
create
Type
StaffAccessManagementStaffGroupController.cs
Staff
Fil
Rettighedd
er
Beskrivelse
Create new StaffGroup
staffGroupName = Name of new Group
accessWebTypesGUID = GUID of WebType from table accesswebtypes
List can be found via /api/StaffAccessManagementStaffGroup/access-web-
types
accessControllerAccessGroupsGUID = GUID of AccessControllerGroups from
table accesscontrolleraccessgroups
List can be found via /api/StaffAccessManagementStaffGroup/access-controller-groups
JSON Request Data
{
"staffGroupName": "StaffGruppe 4",
"accessWebTypesGUID": "66a62d6e-ba1a-11f0-8d44-00155d0a5b1d",
"accessControllerAccessGroupsGUID": "7de2a038-bb05-11f0-8d44-
00155d0a5b1d"
}
JSON Response Data
{
"message": "Staff group created successfully",
"staffGroupGUID": "951f03b5-b39d-4dab-b96f-31f6b0de429a"
}

Navn
Endpoint
Fil
Rettighedd
er
Beskrivelse
Delete
StaffMemberSubscriptionSetOnHold
/api/
Request
StaffMemberSubscriptionSetOnHold/set- Type
hold
StaffMemberSubscriptionSetOnHoldController.cs
Staff
POSTSet an Members Subscription on Hold for a given periode.
Uses settings in the table “organisationsub” field “OrganisationSubJsonData”
so have rules what is allowed.
Settings can be
[{
"ShowMemberCPR":1,
"ShowMemberSex":1,
"ShowMemberHealthInsurance":1,
"MemberAllowCancleSubscription":1,
"MemberAllowHoldSubscription":1,
"MemberAllowHoldSubscriptionType":1,
"MemberAllowHoldSubscriptionMaxPeriode":30,
"MemberAllowHoldSubscriptionFreePeriode":7,
"MemberAllowHoldSubscriptionPrice":2,
"MemberAllowHoldSubscriptionMinReHoldPeriode":90
}]
MemberAllowHoldSubscription = 1 : Member is allowed to set ther
Subscription on hold, 0 : Only staff.
MemberAllowHoldSubscriptionType = 1 : Pay per day, 2 : Fixed price for
periode , 3 : Fixed price per month.
MemberAllowHoldSubscriptionMaxPeriode = Max periode in Dayes a
Subscription can be set on hold.
MemberAllowHoldSubscriptionFreePeriode = Periode it free to set a
Subscription on hold when type is 1, pay per day.
MemberAllowHoldSubscriptionPrice = Price for setting on hold. Can be a
Fixed price or the price per day.
MemberAllowHoldSubscriptionMinReHoldPeriode = The number of dayes
their have to be go from a Subscription hold ended before the can request a
hold again.
memberGuid = GUID of Member
holdStartDate = Start date for hold
holdEndDate = End date for Hold
holdComment = comment why the subscription is set on hold.
JSON Request Body
{
"memberGuid": "b566cdb1-949a-471f-9c61-08fe19f273d2",
"holdStartDate": "2026-05-26T12:45:23.563Z",
"holdEndDate": "2026-06-26T12:45:23.563Z","holdComment": "Test Pause 4"
}
JSON Response Body
{
"message": "Member subscription set on hold successfully",
"memberGuid": "b566cdb1-949a-471f-9c61-08fe19f273d2",
"memberName": "Hans Ny",
"holdPeriod": {
"startDate": "2026-05-26",
"endDate": "2026-06-26",
"totalDays": 31
},
"cost": {
"totalAmount": 48,
"breakdown": [
"Period 2026-05-26 to 2026-05-31: 0,00",
"Period 2026-06-01 to 2026-06-26: 48,00"
],
"type": "Daily billing",
"freePeriod": "7 days free"
},
"emailSent": true,
"paymentRecordsCreated": 2
}
JSON Response Body if Hold is not possible because limits are not excited.
{
"message": "Minimum period between holds not met. Last hold ended on
2026-06-26. Earliest allowed new hold start date is 2026-09-24 (90 days after
last hold)",
"lastHoldEndDate": "2026-06-26",
"earliestAllowedDate": "2026-09-24",
"minReHoldPeriodeDays": 90
}
Ore when more day that allowed.
{
"message": "Hold period (181 days) exceeds maximum allowed period (130
days)"
}Navn
Endpoint
MemberMembershipCancellation (Get Informations)
/api/MemberMembershipCancellation/
Request
earliest-cancellation-date
Type
MemberMembershipCancellationController.cs
Member
GET
Fil
Rettighedd
er
Beskrivelse
Get information about if i member is allowed to cancel their membership by
them self and the rules for the earliest date, they can cancel their
membership from.
Baesed on the settinsg from Center Settings
MemberAllowCancleSubscription = 0 : Member is not allowed to Cancel their
Subscription, 1 : is allowed to Cancel their Subscription
MemberAllowCancleSubscriptionPeriode = Current month plus this number
before a Member can cancel their Subscription
MemberAllowCancleSubscriptionBindingPeriode = Periode in months a
Member have to be Subscribet befor a membership can be candled.
MemberAllowCancleSubscriptionInBindingPeriode:1 = Is the Member
allowed to Cancel their Subscription whele their are in their BindingPeriode,
1 = Yes , 0 = No
VIA API : /api/OrganisationInfo/ShowSettings
earliestCancellationDate is the first date a member can chose to cancel their
membership.
canCancel = Is member allowed to cancel by them self.
JSON Response Data
{
"canCancel": true,
"earliestCancellationDate": "2026-01-01",
"memberCreatedDate": "2025-08-06",
"bindingPeriodMonths": 3,
"noticePeriodMonths": 1,
"canCancelInBindingPeriod": true,
"canCancelNow": false,
"message": "You can cancel your membership starting from 2026-01-01"
}
If members is not allowed to cancel their memberships by themself the
message isJSON Response Body
{
"message": "Membership cancellation is not allowed for this organization",
"canCancel": false
}
If a cancellation is already mad the result is
JSON Request Body
{
"message": "A cancellation request is already pending for this membership"
}

Endpoint
MemberMembershipCancellation (Cancel Membeship)
/api/MemberMembershipCancellation/
Request
POST
cancel-membership
Type
MemberMembershipCancellationController.cs
Fil
Rettighedd
er
Beskrivelse
API for e member to cancel their Membership is they allowed to by the
Center Settings.
Requered Data
cancellationDate = The date the cancelation should happen.
cancellationReason = The text why the member shoes I cancel their
membership.
The check from MemberMembershipCancellation (Get Informations) is
made before to ensure member is allowed to cancel and the Cancel date is
allowed.
JSON Request Data
{
"cancellationDate": "2026-01-01",
"cancellationReason": "Gider ikke mere"
}
JSON Response Data on success
{
"message": "Membership cancellation request submitted successfully",
"cancellationGuid": "5e64ba71-b9f8-434a-bd90-b8c4cec55e8d","cancellationDate": "2026-01-01",
"emailSent": true
}
JSON Response Data if the date is to early
{
"message": "Cancellation date cannot be earlier than 2026-01-01",
"earliestAllowedDate": "2026-01-01"
}

Endpoint
StaffMembershipCancellation (Cancel Member)
/api/StaffMembershipCancellation/
Request
cancel-membership
Type
POSTFil
StaffMembershipCancellationController.cs
Rettighedd Staff
er
Beskrivelse
Cancel a members membership.
It follows the normal Cancellation rules for the data a membership can be
Cancelled.
But the Staff has an Option to overwrite the rules id necessary.
memberGuid = GUDI of member
cancellationDate = Date of the cancellation
cancellationReason = The reason of the cancellation
cancellationOverride = True to override the normal rules of cancellation
Request Body Data
{
"memberGuid": "d89e313d-e036-4d4e-84e1-6d706848816d",
"cancellationDate": "2025-12-01",
"cancellationReason": "Han skal ud med det samme",
"cancellationOverride": true
}
Else if cancellationOverride = false
{
"message": "Cancellation date cannot be earlier than 2026-01-01. Use
cancellationOverride to bypass this restriction.",
"earliestAllowedDate": "2026-01-01"
}
